Please note: exactly same process is used for each of the domain library\\n212: \\n213: The git tag for a release candidate must follow the following format:\\n214: ```\\n215: v{MAJOR}.{MINOR}.{PATCH}-rc{RC_NUMBER}\\n216: ```\\n217: \\n218: An example of this would look like:\\n219: ```\\n220: v1.12.0-rc1\\n221: ```\\n222: You can use following commands to perform tag from pytorch core repo (not fork):\\n223: * Checkout and validate the repo history before tagging\\n224: ```\\n225: git checkout release/1.12\\n226: git log --oneline\\n227: ```\\n228: * Perform tag and push it to github (this will trigger the binary release build)\\n229: ```\\n230: git tag -f  v1.12.0-rc2\\n231: git push origin  v1.12.0-rc2\\n232: ```\\n233: \\n234: Pushing a release candidate tag should trigger the `binary_build` workflows.
